data-component="Standfirst">US Secretary of State Mike Pompeo says there is &quot;a significant amount of evidence&quot; that the new coronavirus emerged from a Chinese laboratory, but also says he agrees with US intelligence agencies who say it is not man-made.</p><section class="key-points__section--2ybzm key-points__borders--Es5LH content-alignment__margin-bottom--1LbdU content-alignment__overflow-auto--1bAUU content-alignment__float-right--q-cWK" role="contentinfo" aria-label="key points" data-component="KeyPoints"><h2 class="typography__size-mobile-18--zT1nT typography__size-desktop-20--4Zpdk typography__line-height-mobile-24--SelAj typography__margin-bottom-mobile-small--1t9H3 typography__line-height-desktop-24--2-MxD typography__margin-bottom-desktop-small--lxkD- typography__black--mSYxO typography__colour-inherit--age8P" data-component="Heading">Key points:</h2><ul class="list__unordered--3Crv1" data-component="List"><li class="" data-component="ListItem"><span class="list-item__bullet--1HQd4 list-item__square--as_Ss"></span>Donald Trump has suggested COVID-19 may have originated in a Chinese virology lab</li><li class="" data-component="ListItem"><span class="list-item__bullet--1HQd4 list-item__square--as_Ss"></span>The Wuhan Institute of Virology has dismissed allegations against it</li><li class="" data-component="ListItem"><span class="list-item__bullet--1HQd4 list-item__square--as_Ss"></span>Intelligence reports say &quot;the wide scientific consensus&quot; is that COVID-19 was not man-made</li></ul></section><p>&quot;There is a significant amount of evidence that this came from that laboratory in Wuhan,&quot; Mr Pompeo told ABC America&#x27;s This Week.</p><p>Mr Pompeo then briefly contradicted a statement issued this week by the top US spy agency that said the virus did not appear to be man-made or genetically modified. </p><p>That statement undercut conspiracy theories promoted by anti-China activists and some supporters of President Donald Trump who suggested it was developed in a Chinese government biological weapons laboratory.</p><aside class="content-alignment__margin-bottom--1LbdU content-alignment__overflow-auto--1bAUU pullquote__pullquote--3nAF7" data-component="Pullquote"><blockquote class="pullquote__quote--OsWT8"><p>&quot;The best experts so far seem to think it was man-made. I have no reason to disbelieve that at this point,&quot; Mr Pompeo said. </p></blockquote></aside><aside class="content-alignment__margin-bottom--1LbdU content-alignment__overflow-auto--1bAUU legacy-wysiwyg__wysiwyg--34JiP" data-component="LegacyWysiwyg"><a class="link__link--2HoMm link__visited--31PBK link__focus--34Pu4" href="https://www.abc.net.au/news/2020-05-05/coronavirus-update-australia-covid19-russia-italy-australia/12213200" data-component="ContentLink">Coronavirus update: Follow all the latest news in our daily wrap</a></aside><aside class="content-alignment__margin-bottom--1LbdU content-alignment__overflow-auto--1bAUU content-alignment__float-right--q-cWK related-card__related-card--17_v7" data-component="RelatedCard"><a class="media-object__card-link-default--11xOR link__link--2HoMm link__visited--31PBK link__underline-none--3dlTb link__black--1UYpe" href="https://www.abc.net.au/radio/programs/coronacast/latest-segments/12025304" data-component="MediaObject"><div class="media-object__media-object--1nvz- media-object__media-object-vertical--1EB8Y media-object__title-first--dJVU3"><h3 class="typography__size-mobile-18--zT1nT typography__size-desktop-20--4Zpdk typography__line-height-mobile-24--SelAj typography__margin-bottom-mobile-small--1t9H3 typography__line-height-desktop-24--2-MxD typography__margin-bottom-desktop-small--lxkD- typography__black--mSYxO typography__colour-inherit--age8P media-object__header--12_JB media-object__break--36Roe" data-component="Heading"><span>Coronavirus questions answered</span></h3><div class="media-object__image-container--1-32G"><amp-img layout="responsive" class="content-image__amp-image--1bTp0 related-card__image--1oHNh" alt="An illustration of a cell on an orange background with the word &#x27;coronacast&#x27; overlayed." src="https://www.abc.net.au/cm/lb/12027368/data/coronacast-pic-teaser-data.jpg" width="1.7777777777777777" height="1" data-component="Image"></amp-img><p class="typography__size-mobile-12--3Jwd8 typography__line-height-mobile-24--SelAj typography__bold--oTwkj typography__colour-inherit--age8P related-card__synopsis--3oS1C" data-component="Typography">Breaking down the latest news and research to understand how the world is living through an epidemic, this is the ABC&#x27;s Coronacast podcast.</p><span class="related-card__more-link--18E0r"><span class="typography__size-mobile-14--2wxqg typography__line-height-mobile-24--SelAj typography__bold--oTwkj typography__colour-inherit--age8P" data-component="Typography">Read more</span><svg class="related-card__icon--14QEG icon__size-20--2HqIc" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="20" height="20" data-component="Icon" aria-hidden="true"><use xlink:href="#dls-icon-arrow-right"></use></svg></span></div></div></a></aside><p>When the interviewer pointed out that was not the conclusion of US intelligence agencies, Mr Pompeo backtracked, and said: &quot;I&#x27;ve seen what the intelligence community has said. I have no reason to believe that they&#x27;ve got it wrong.&quot;</p><p>The US State Department did not immediately respond to a request for clarification on Mr Pompeo&#x27;s comments.</p><p>Thursday&#x27;s report from the Office of the Director of National Intelligence said it concurred with &quot;the wide scientific consensus&quot; that the disease was not man-made.</p><p>US officials familiar with intelligence reporting and analysis have said for weeks that they do not believe Chinese scientists developed the new coronavirus in a government biological weapons lab from which it then escaped.</p><figure class="figure__figure--3M2Ue content-alignment__margin-bottom--1LbdU content-alignment__overflow-auto--1bAUU content-alignment__overflow-auto--1bAUU legacy-wysiwyg__wysiwyg--34JiP" data-component="LegacyWysiwyg"><a id="remove"></a><figure class="figure__figure--3M2Ue content-alignment__margin-bottom--1LbdU I&#x27;m not allowed to tell you that,&quot; Mr Trump said.</p></blockquote></aside><p>The Chinese state-backed Wuhan Institute of Virology has dismissed the allegations, and other US officials have downplayed their likelihood.</p><p>Most experts believe the virus originated in a market selling wildlife in Wuhan and jumped from animals to people.</p><aside class="content-alignment__margin-bottom--1LbdU content-alignment__overflow-auto--1bAUU legacy-wysiwyg__wysiwyg--34JiP" data-component="LegacyWysiwyg"><h2 class="typography__size-mobile-20--1LI2A
